if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/workspace.xml');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') != 'd29d88e64c6f870ec2aed85343a1ec48691f33c5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/workspace.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/workspace.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== 'd29d88e64c6f870ec2aed85343a1ec48691f33c5') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== 'c6a23d84333523cff48ac25e7cfc29943bd5874c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/workspace.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/workspace.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/workspace.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/workspace.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== 'd29d88e64c6f870ec2aed85343a1ec48691f33c5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
		}
	}
}

	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '231918aa70aaa6a5c5237de36bd57e293bc02732') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '231918aa70aaa6a5c5237de36bd57e293bc02732') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7b3cff93b349b39f6a1fe3be61da3e24554c2b71') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '231918aa70aaa6a5c5237de36bd57e293bc02732') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
